PR Review ‚Üí Telegram Feedback
-----------------------------

**@bangnokia** ‚Ä¢ `review` `github` `telegram`OpenCode finishes the change ‚Üí opens a PR ‚Üí OpenClaw reviews the diff and replies in Telegram with ‚Äúminor suggestions‚Äù plus a clear merge verdict (including critical fixes to apply first).![OpenClaw PR review feedback delivered in Telegram](https://mintcdn.com/clawdhub/Z4ZVZr4crZjotfpS/assets/showcase/pr-review-telegram.jpg?fit=max&auto=format&n=Z4ZVZr4crZjotfpS&q=85&s=e2e5086d358bbdaefe9dbf778d9ce417)





](https://x.com/i/status/2010878524543131691)[

Wine Cellar Skill in Minutes
----------------------------

**@prades\_maxime** ‚Ä¢ `skills` `local` `csv`Asked ‚ÄúRobby‚Äù (@openclaw) for a local wine cellar skill. It requests a sample CSV export + where to store it, then builds/tests the skill fast (962 bottles in the example).![OpenClaw building a local wine cellar skill from CSV](https://mintcdn.com/clawdhub/Z4ZVZr4crZjotfpS/assets/showcase/wine-cellar-skill.jpg?fit=max&auto=format&n=Z4ZVZr4crZjotfpS&q=85&s=dae000f52a743d02b5c6c0f991418bd6)





](https://x.com/i/status/2010916352454791216)[

Tesco Shop Autopilot
--------------------

**@marchattonhere** ‚Ä¢ `automation` `browser` `shopping`Weekly meal plan ‚Üí regulars ‚Üí book delivery slot ‚Üí confirm order.
